The `shouldUseESMLoader` function checks these conditions, and if ESM is needed, it calls `runEntryPointWithESMLoader` which initializes the cascaded loader.\\n\\n## Core ESM Loader (lib/internal/modules/esm/loader.js)\\nThe `ModuleLoader` class is the central machinery for module loading. It maintains:\\n- `#resolveCache`: Registry of resolved specifiers (ResolveCache from module_map.js)\\n- `loadCache`: Registry of loaded modules (LoadCache)\\n- `translators`: Methods that translate input code into ES modules\\n- `#customizations`: For custom user-defined loader hooks\\n\\nThe ModuleLoader exposes `import()`, `resolve()`, and `load()` methods that coordinate the two-phase loading process.\\n\\n## Specifier Resolution (lib/internal/modules/esm/resolve.js)\\nThe `defaultResolve` function implements the core resolution algorithm that converts module specifiers into absolute URLs. It handles:\\n- Built-in modules (node:)\\n- Relative paths (./,  ../)\\n- Absolute URLs\\n- Package exports resolution via packageExportsResolve\\n- Package imports resolution via packageImportsResolve\\n\\n## Module Format Detection (lib/internal/modules/esm/get_format.js)\\nThe `defaultGetFormat` function determines module format based on:\\n- File extension (.js, .mjs, .cjs, .json, .wasm)\\n- MIME type for data: URLs\\n- Package.json type field\\n- --experimental-default-type flag\\n- Syntax detection for ambiguous .js files\\n\\n## Source Loading detection when needed\\n- Source validation\\n\\n## Module Translation (lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js)\\nThe `translators` map contains strategies for different formats:\\n- 'module': Standard JavaScript modules compiled to ModuleWrap\\n- 'json': JSON imports with validations\\n- 'wasm': WebAssembly modules\\n- 'commonjs': CommonJS modules via CJS facade\\n- 'builtin': Built-in Node modules\\n- 'commonjs-sync': Synchronous CommonJS loading for require() in ESM\\n\\n## Module Job Pipeline (lib/internal/modules/esm/module_job.js)\\nThe `ModuleJob` class tracks module loading lifecycle:\\n- Constructor takes loader, URL, import attributes, and module promise\\n- Manages linking via `_link()` that recursively processes dependencies\\n- Handles evaluation through `_evaluate()`\\n- Implements error handling for cycles and async issues\\n- `ModuleJobBase` provides base properties for both async and sync variants\\n\\n## Module Caching (lib/internal/modules/esm/module_map.js)\\nTwo cache layers:\\n- `ResolveCache`: Caches resolution results per (specifier, parentURL, importAttributes)\\n- `LoadCache`: Caches the final result of load-chain for each module URL\\n\\n## Custom Loader Hooks (lib/internal/modules/esm/hooks.js)\\nThe `Hooks` class manages custom loader chains:\\n- Maintains resolve and load hook chains as LIFO queues\\n- Each hook receives the result from the previous one\\n- Integrates with worker thread for hook execution\\n- Validates hook return values\\n\\n## Dynamic Module Creation (lib/internal/modules/esm/create_dynamic_module.js)\\nThe `createDynamicModule` function generates synthetic ESM modules with:\\n- Dynamic import/export support\\n- Custom evaluation via with:\\n- `url`: Module URL\\n- `dirname` and `filename`: For file: URLs only\\n- `resolve`: Function for import.meta.resolve() when enabled\\n\\n## CJS-ESM Interop resolution\\n- Validates encoded characters in resolved URL\\n- Returns the finalized file path\\n\\n## Native ModuleWrap Binding (src/module_wrap.h, src/module_wrap.cc)\\nThe C++ `ModuleWrap` class provides:\\n- V8 Module compilation and caching\\n- Module instantiation and evaluation\\n- Top-level await checking\\n- Import attribute tracking\\n- Synchronous and asynchronous linking/evaluation\\n- Module status queries\\n- Cache data generation for faster subsequent loads\\n\\n## Module Modules Binding (src/node_modules.cc)\\nProvides package.json caching and resolution (lib/internal/modules/esm/worker.js)\\nManages custom loader execution in isolated worker:\\n- Synchronous communication via SharedArrayBuffer\\n- Hook registration and invocation\\n- Error
